[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered via the Apple MakerNote loader [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_load`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing a specially crafted input.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The crash is classified as a heap-buffer-overflow: a one‐byte read past the end [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof a heap allocation.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observed Behavior  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While running the fuzzer in interactive mode with libFuzzer and ASan enabled, the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall stack shows:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `exif_get_sshort` attempts to read beyond a [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m‐byte buffer.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. This is invoked by `exif_get_short` in exif-utils.c.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Next up the stack is `exif_mnote_data_apple_load` [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mapple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which parses Apple-specific MakerNote entries.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The loader is called by the generic parser `exif_data_load_data` → [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_new_from_data`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Finally, `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` serves as the entry point for the fuzzer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  AddressSanitizer reports the invalid read at an address [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes past the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region’s end, indicating a parsing routine is indexing beyond the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovided data buffer.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow arises during EXIF “short” value extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_get_sshort`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The buffer in question is allocated by the fuzzer harness to hold test input.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash consistently reproduces under libFuzzer with `-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The vulnerability occurs in the core libexif parsing logic, not in the harness [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mitself.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • exif-utils.c – implementation of `exif_get_sshort` and related byte‐order [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c – how MakerNote entries are indexed and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidated.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • exif-data.c – overall data loading routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_data_load_data` and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_new_from_data`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_from_data_fuzzer.cc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for how input is handed off to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor context, though not the root cause[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m121[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m122[0m[39m:                                  [0m[32m"ExifMnoteApplet"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Tag size overflow [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mdetected [0m[32m([0m[32m%u vs size %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, dofs, buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m123[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mcontinue;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m124[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/exif-format.[0m[1;92mc:37[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m44[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mEXIF_FORMAT_SHORT,     [0m[1;35mN_[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Short"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,     [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mEXIF_FORMAT_UNDEFINED, [0m[1;35mN_[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Undefined"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mEXIF_FORMAT_LONG,      [0m[1;35mN_[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Long"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,      [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mEXIF_FORMAT_BYTE,      [0m[1;35mN_[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Byte"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,      [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:     [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mEXIF_FORMAT_SBYTE,     [0m[1;35mN_[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"SByte"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,     [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In libexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c, after computing the data size [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`dsize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the data offset within the MakerNote block [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dofs`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code only [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks that the start offset [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dofs`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is within the buffer:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdofs > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[39m* skip entry *[0m[35m/[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It neglects to verify that the entire range `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdofs, dofs + dsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` lies within[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe buffer. When `dsize == [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m`, and `dofs == buf_size - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, the existing check [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpasses but reading two bytes overruns by one byte, triggering the ASan-reported [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow in `exif_get_sshort`.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy for Safe Bounds Checking[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mirror the pattern used in the generic MakerNote loader [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`libexif/exif-mnote-data.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which enforces:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry_ofs + entry_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           continue;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the single-offset check in the Apple-specific loader with a combined [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck that the end offset does not exceed `buf_size`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To avoid integer wrap-around issues, prefer the pattern:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdsize > buf_size || dofs > buf_size - dsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[39m* log overflow and skip *[0m[35m/[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This ensures `dofs + dsize` cannot overflow the address space and that the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull data window is valid.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `libexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c`.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the loop processing each entry [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m115[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m124[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```c[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       dsize = [0m[1;35mexif_format_get_size[0m[1;39m([0m[39md->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39md->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.components;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdsize > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           dofs = d->offset + [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + ofs + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, d->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           dofs = ofs + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdofs > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Tag size overflow detected [0m[32m([0m[32m%u vs size %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, dofs, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           continue;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Replace the single-offset check with a combined bounds check:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```c[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Ensure the entire data window [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdofs, dofs + dsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fits in buf_size *[0m[35m/[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdsize > buf_size || dofs > buf_size - dsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    [0m[32m"ExifMnoteApplet"[0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    [0m[32m"Tag size overflow detected [0m[32m([0m[32moffset %u + size %u > buffer %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    dofs, dsize, buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           continue;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Keep the original `exif_mnote_data_append` call unmodified so it safely [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopies exactly `dsize` bytes.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change only tightens the boundary check. It does not alter parsing logic, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry-count iteration, or data-copy mechanisms.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, fuzzing logic, or other source files are modified, ensuring [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests and the libFuzzer harness continue to function unchanged.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The log message is extended slightly to include both offset and size, aiding [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuture diagnostics without changing semantics.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new check may skip more malformed entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthose that would have [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mover‐read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Existing code already skipped entries on start‐offset overflow, so this[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly increases safety.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance impact beyond a simple extra subtraction and comparison per [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer arithmetic uses unsigned types; the pattern `dofs > buf_size - dsize` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevents wrap‐around, so no undefined behavior is introduced.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Conclusion[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This patch fully addresses the one‐byte heap‐buffer‐overflow in the Apple [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMakerNote loader by rigorously validating the data window before any read [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation. It aligns the Apple‐specific code with the generic loader’s robust [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary‐checking pattern and preserves all existing functionality and testing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharnesses.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change rationale: ensure both the declared data size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dsize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fits in buffer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand that the offset plus size does not surpass `buf_size`.[0m                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Still crashes at `exif_get_sshort` reading beyond the allocated [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m-byte [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - The stack trace and overflow offset are identical to the original failure.[0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintercept the out-of-bounds scenario before `exif_get_sshort` is called.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Further Investigation[0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m189[0m[39m:    return d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.tag;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m190[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m191[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:static const char *[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m193:e[0m[1;35mxif_mnote_data_apple_get_name[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *md, unsigned int i[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:    ExifMnoteDataApple *d = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteDataApple *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m md;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!d || [0m[1;39m([0m[39md->count <= i[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:        return NULL;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:    return [0m[1;35mmnote_apple_tag_get_name[0m[1;39m([0m[39md->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.tag[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/exif-mnote-data.[0m[1;92mc:158[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m158[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m158[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.[0m[1;92mc:85[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m95[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:    tcount = [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mexif_get_short[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + ofs + [0m[1;36m14[0m[39m, d->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Sanity check the offset *[0m[35m/[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m + tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:                 [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short MakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m[1;35mprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"%s[0m[32m([0m[32m%d[0m[32m)[0m[32m\n"[0m[39m, __FUNCTION__, __LINE__[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;*[0m[35m/[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m:        return;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m94[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m95[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* [0m[1;35mprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"%s[0m[32m([0m[32m%d[0m[32m)[0m[32m: total %d tags\n"[0m[39m, __FUNCTION__, __LINE__, tcount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; *[0m[35m/[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Apple maker-note loader’s “sanity check” before iterating directory [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries uses “tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m” bytes as the required space, but each entry is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactually [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bytes long [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte tag + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte format + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte component count + [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m-byte offset/inline data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This underestimation lets truncated buffers pass the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck, then the loop unconditionally calls exif_get_short/long at buf+ofs, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflowing when ‘ofs’ is near buf_size.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - exif_get_sshort [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand exif_get_short[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m perform unguarded reads of two bytes, so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many call with less than two bytes remaining in the buffer will trigger an [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds read.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve & Reapply Existing Patch[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain the previously added bounds check on “dofs” and “dsize” in the loop [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mthe `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdsize > buf_size || dofs > buf_size - dsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so that payload [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopies stay safe.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Update Directory-Size Sanity Check[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove or replace the old check at lines [0m[1;36m87[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m93[0m[39m:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m + tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short MakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately after computing the first entry offset [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ofs += [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecise check ensuring all tcount entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39meach [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fit:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Ensure directory entries are fully contained in buffer *[0m[35m/[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < ofs + tcount * [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                     [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                     [0m[32m"MakerNote directory overflow: %u entries exceed buffer %u"[0m[39m,[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                     tcount, buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This guarantees that the subsequent loop’s calls to exif_get_short/long at [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuf+ofs…buf+ofs+[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m are within bounds.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Optional Per-Entry Safety Guard[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIf further hardening is desired[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m At the top of each loop iteration, verify [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ofs <= buf_size - [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m` before reading the tag/format/components:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mofs > buf_size - [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"MakerNote entry header overflow"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            break;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This secondary guard prevents any remaining underflows if future code changes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshift the initial sanity check.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Side-Effects[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using an exact `tcount * [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m` calculation aligns with the TIFF‐style directory [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat and matches the checks performed by other maker-note loaders in the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserving the existing dsize/dofs patch ensures payload copies remain safe; [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe new check closes the earlier oversight in header parsing.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, utility, or external library code is modified; test coverage and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting functionality are maintained.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential minor performance impact is negligible, as it replaces a lightweight[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marithmetic check.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar directory‐size bounds checks exist in Nikon/Olympus loaders—this [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange harmonizes Apple loader behavior with those proven implementations.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In libexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c, locate the block around the tcount [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      tcount = [0m[1;35mexif_get_short[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + ofs + [0m[1;36m14[0m[39m, d->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m* old sanity check: buf_size < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m+[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m + tcount*[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ofs += [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m* loop over entries *[0m[35m/[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Remove the old `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m + tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Immediately after `ofs += [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;` insert:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < ofs + tcount * [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m,[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   [0m[32m"MakerNote directory overflow: %u entries exceed buffer %u"[0m[39m,[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   tcount, buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Keep the loop’s existing patch for data‐offset vs. payload‐size checks [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintact.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Build and re-run the fuzzer; the heap-buffer-overflow in exif_get_sshort [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould no longer trigger, as both header reads and payload copies are fully [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidated.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                   [0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.END                      ]8;id=53901;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=425673;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
